  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_194e92e5-f68a-423e-a812-1eb55d3780b3'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText15901015123364880101" style="display:none"><b>Some loves will last ’til your dying breath</b><br /><br />Every choice has consequences—but seventeen-year-old Layla faces tougher choices than most. Light or darkness. Wickedly sexy demon prince Roth, or Zayne, the gorgeous, protective Warden she never thought could be hers. Hardest of all, Layla has to decide which side of herself to trust.<br /><br />Layla has a new problem, too. A Lilin—the deadliest of demons—has been unleashed, wreaking havoc on those around her…including her best friend. To keep Sam from a fate much, much worse than death, Layla must strike a deal with the enemy while saving her city—and her race—from destruction.<br /><br />Torn between two worlds and two different boys, Layla has no certainties, least of all survival, especially when an old bargain comes back to haunt them all. But sometimes, when secrets are everywhere and the truth seems unknowable, you have to listen to your heart, pick a side—and then fight like hell…</span>

</a>'s blurb. <br><br>Like my profile says, I <s>absolutely</s> fucking <b>loathe love triangles</b>.<br><br><a href="http://it.tinypic.com?ref=2i24lxt" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <i>The Dark Elements<i></i></i>
</a> isn't one of them because of the shit I've read on her <a href="http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/the-choice-is-in-your-hands/" rel="nofollow noopener">site</a>.<br><br><a href="http://it.tinypic.com?ref=vi19pw" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Unlike anyone too. (Or at least, I hope so.)<br><br><a href="http://it.tinypic.com?ref=2lvicsj" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

She IS the writer, not us. I loved her polls, till today. It's one thing to let readers decide a book's title or a character's name and it's completely another to let them decide about the story/plot/book/whatever itself. <br><br>We all know <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455815-stone-cold-touch" rel="nofollow noopener">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1105608780" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16393486189598557100"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438793135i/15755095._SX540_.jpg' alt='https://www.google.com/search?hl=en' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Every Last Breath by Jennifer L. Armentrout is the third and final book in the series The Dark Elements. Holy Canola Oil and Wow, just Wow! This book was amazing! There were no down times, no slow spots, just amazing from page one until the end. And what a fantastic ending it was. <br/><br/>This is going to be one of those reviews where I am so limited as to what I can say without spoiling anything. Things start right where the previous book left off. The Lilin has taken over Layla’s friend Sam’s body. Bu</span>
  <span id="freeText16393486189598557100" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438793135i/15755095._SX540_.jpg" alt="https://www.google.com/search?hl=en" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Every Last Breath by Jennifer L. Armentrout is the third and final book in the series The Dark Elements. Holy Canola Oil and Wow, just Wow! This book was amazing! There were no down times, no slow spots, just amazing from page one until the end. And what a fantastic ending it was. <br><br>This is going to be one of those reviews where I am so limited as to what I can say without spoiling anything. Things start right where the previous book left off. The Lilin has taken over Layla’s friend Sam’s body. But not just taken over, he has taken his soul. Layla, of course, feels like this is all somehow her fault, and that she alone is responsible for rescuing Sam’s soul from Hell.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/heaven_zps95331b49.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396219891i/9103331.jpg" alt=" photo heaven_zps95331b49.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Layla is also still filled with guilt over what happened between she and Zayne. She knows that she can’t continue on this way, that she must decide between these two men who are so important to her. Who really does hold her heart? Who is she truly in love with? The beautiful gargoyle shifter that she has loved since she was seven years old or the dark and brooding Crown Prince who looks at her with a longing she might never really understand. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438793135i/15755096._SY540_.jpg" alt="https://www.tumblr.com/search/every last breath" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Layla starts to notice subtle changes in herself. She isn’t craving souls the way she used to. She’s not cold the way she was. She’s a little faster, and a little stronger. And when she shifts, well, wow! What is happening and what does it all mean? There are many questions as to who and what Layla really is and all questions are answered. <br><br><b>
  <i>“As I parted ways with Stacey, I knew that my promise had done very little to reassure her. Truth was, the promise was one I never should’ve made. Because I had a lot of stupid left in me, and I knew what I had to do.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438793135i/15755097._SY540_.jpg" alt="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/photos/pb.285190961582473.-2207520000.1438737949./681094005325498/?type=3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Lilin wants Lilith set free and if she is, she will bring on devastation to the world. If she isn’t set free, the Originals will come and do the same. And of course, all the responsibility of figuring all of this out rests on Layla’s shoulders. <br><br><b>
  <i>“What was happening was so much bigger than us, so much more important than what we wanted or desired.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438793135i/15755098._SX540_.jpg" alt="https://www.google.com/search?hl=en" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is so much Layla want to do. She wants to finish high school, go to college. She wants to travel. She’s never been anywhere. She has never been accepted by the clan who raised her, been rejected by those that created her. So why does she feel responsible to fix everything? She could run, go somewhere and hide. But the Layla we have all fallen in love with won’t do that. She’ll fight for what she feels is right, no matter what the sacrifice. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438793135i/15755099._SY540_.jpg" alt="https://www.google.com/search?hl=en" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This whole series was amazing and the ending was epic. I expected no less. This is Jennifer Armentrout and everything I have read of hers has been equally wonderful and unique. This book will keep you on the edge of your seat from the beginning to the end. But as much as there is ugliness in Layla’s world, there is beauty. She is in love. I sighed so much during this book that I might have hyperventilated. I have to say thank you again to JLA for a wonderfully entertaining series. I don’t know where all your creativity comes from, but I thank you for it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425952445ra/13954015.gif" alt="signature" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16393486189598557100" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1194188263" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1194188263" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30035966-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523817330p2/30035966.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1194188263?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/30035966-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=badass-females">badass-females</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=5-star-favorites">5-star-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1194188263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10625858985751362519">It's been a long time since I've gotten behind the wheel of a Jla book, and it's been a long time since I devoured a book this fast. Started it at 3 finished it at five. <i>Every Last Breath </i>is the third and final book in the <i>Dark Elements Trilogy</i>, if you haven't read the first two please do not pass go and do not pick up two-hundred dollars. GO BACK NOW AND READ THE FIRST TWO!!!! <i>Every Last Breath </i>does not let down.<br/><br/>As much as I want to load this review with spoils that would turn you rotten I wont</span>
  <span id="freeText10625858985751362519" style="display:none">It's been a long time since I've gotten behind the wheel of a Jla book, and it's been a long time since I devoured a book this fast. Started it at 3 finished it at five. <i>Every Last Breath </i>is the third and final book in the <i>Dark Elements Trilogy</i>, if you haven't read the first two please do not pass go and do not pick up two-hundred dollars. GO BACK NOW AND READ THE FIRST TWO!!!! <i>Every Last Breath </i>does not let down.<br><br>As much as I want to load this review with spoils that would turn you rotten I wont.<br><i>ELB </i>picks up right where <i>Stone Cold Touch </i>left off. The Lilin is still out and causing chaos. Layla is still confused about what she is. And of course we are still waiting on the answer of who the hell does Layla pick. Gargoyle Zayne or Crown Prince of the Under World Roth... I like everyone else mainly was waiting to find out which dude she be choosin. Clearly being team Roth I was on the edge of my seating waiting for the moment when the big question was answered... And boy do we get an answer. No I wont tell you what happens... I will give you (of course) a run-down of what I thought.<br><br>Layla is still one of my favorite Fems and brings the thunder in this book. Finally putting on her big girl panties I was so happy with her character development. She goes from a strong physical character, to a strong emotional character. She starts making decisions and realizes becoming an adult means having to make tough choices, but you have to make them. Good or bad outcome it must be done. Then we have sweet sweet Zayne. Who again continues to be a strong male presence and someone you want to cheer for... Even if deep down inside, in this case, you'll want the nice guy to finish last... <i>sorry</i>. I overall liked his character in this book, even though at one point I did think the direction something was taken was a little cheese. On to Roth... <b>HOLY HOT DEMON BABIES EVERYWHERE ROTH... WHOOSH... SWOON! I'd walk through hell for his hottie! He blew my mind in this book. </b>Didn't think it was possible for him to get any better, but yup WRONG. Every time he was present I had to make sure I was sitting down; just got so weak in the knees. If getting pregnant by reading was possible... Well I wouldn't need Maury to tell me that Roth IS the father.<br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qHR2FBtb7iI/VbgCB5ftsbI/AAAAAAAACCg/xjdfdzyta68/s1600/pregnant.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img height="208" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438123773ra/15667360.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br><b>"</b><i>
  <b>And my desire for you increases every waking second in a way that should frighten me, but really just excites me. But most of all, I love you... Yesterday. Today. Tomorrow, a hundred decades from now, I will still be in love with you..." </b>
</i><br><br>I thought Layla had a lot of growth, but she has nothing on Roth. I will give this tiny bit of information... There is a drunk Roth scene and oh Lord did I love it!!! He was on my list of favorite fictional guys but has definitely moved up. On too my favorite topic when it comes to Jla books. Yes, her side characters! Jla write some of my favorite side characters. Doesn't matter how big or small their rolls are I always love them. My two favorites hands down were Tony the seer who happens to require you to bring him dinner when you visit and Cayman, Roth's right hand man. Both had my sides splitting! Especially Cayman. I didn't remember loving him so much <i>Stone Cold Touch</i>, but he loved him so much in <i>Every Last Breath</i>. Every sarcastic sentence that oozed from his mouth was perfection. Every character in this book is so easily liked.<br><br>The plot of this book went very different than I thought. It was a lot heavier on the smushy romance (no this isn't a complaint) and saved a lot of the action for the last half of this book. Knowing this was surrounding a love triangle I knew there was going to be a lot of smutty goodness but had no idea what I was in for!  I was actually happy with how this played out, because I wont lie I was worried. I think if anyone else besides Jla would have attempted to do such heavy romance and hold off on the action till the end it might not have played out as well. When the action does come, though a tiny bit predictable, still hit home and cuts deep. I again wont lie, though I wanted action, that wasn't why I choose this book. I choose it because I knew it was going to be a fun, hilarious, romantic read, with a well written triangle. Going into it wanting that and then getting it has me left completely stratified with the ending to this wondering and different paranormal trilogy. I highly recommend this series. Was getting in a bit of a slump and as usual Jennifer pulled me right back out. This was the perfect summer romance read. <br><br><b><br>READ THIS REVIEW AND OTHERS OVER ON OUR BLOG:<br><br><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">SOUTHERN BRED SOUTHER READ </a><br><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">SOUTHERN BRED SOUTHER READ  </a><br><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">SOUTHERN BRED SOUTHER READ </a><br><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">SOUTHERN BRED SOUTHER READ  </a></b></span>

<div id="review_977866934" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/977866934" />
    <a title="Taschima" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2435020-taschima"><img alt="Taschima" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574541558p2/2435020.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/977866934?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taschima" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taschima" href="/user/show/2435020-taschima">Taschima</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer977866934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9832655033534442467">I realized something while reading Every Last Breath, I was in it for the romance. I was in it for the will she choose Roth? Or Zayne? Will we get more smexy scenes? Give me my angsty romance-indecision fix!<br/><br/>LET'S BE REAL: I wasn't in it for the plot, not really, while I thought the relationship between the characters was super entertaining when it came to the world development I realized that it isn't that original or even that interesting. The bad guys aren't even that bad, to be honest. <br/><br/>And on</span>
  <span id="freeText9832655033534442467" style="display:none">I realized something while reading Every Last Breath, I was in it for the romance. I was in it for the will she choose Roth? Or Zayne? Will we get more smexy scenes? Give me my angsty romance-indecision fix!<br /><br />LET'S BE REAL: I wasn't in it for the plot, not really, while I thought the relationship between the characters was super entertaining when it came to the world development I realized that it isn't that original or even that interesting. The bad guys aren't even that bad, to be honest. <br /><br />And once that was all done with? (she decides within like 100 pages of starting the book) Well then, I started really looking into the plot and realized something: I was bored. Demon comes out of hell and wants to destroy the world, the demon has mother issues, blah blah. Also, did anyone notice how the demons of this story are all basically huge puddles of cuddle? I've been watching Supernatural (again, for the hundreth time) while reading this book and I realized something, I like my demons to be, well, evil. Roth is a huge puddle of sexy and good intentions (even though he may not care about anyone's opinion and speaks his mind, that doesn't make him evil--I never once saw him skin someone alive). Isn't he supposed to be the Crown Prince of Hell? The "Boss" as they call the devil is surely slacking. <br /><br />The dialogue is as smooth as always (even with its cringe worth moments of cheesyness-- some of which Layla even points out as being the ultimate of cheese, but does that negate the moment?) and it takes no time at all to go through the book. There are plenty of steamy scenes, even the obligatory "gentle taking of your precious virginity" scene. But, I also noticed something, while I may be all into Roth, my favorite sexy scene of this series involves Zayne (when they are in bed together and he is all tracing the snake in book 2). Go figure.<br /><br />There are also some pretty cool battle scenes, where Layla gets to show off her FEATHERED wings (don't forget, they have FEATHERS). There is also this particular scene where Layla goes toe to toe with the Lilin at the end... I really liked that scene. It stands out in my mind.<br /><br />As far as the ending is concern, well, I don't buy it. It ended with the biggest and prettiest red bow. Everything fell into place so perfectly... making sure no FEATHERS were ruffled and no fan rages against the machine. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I am supposed to believe the DEVIL brings her back out of the goodness of her heart? Because the devil ALSO cares for Roth? Ugh, give me a break THIS IS LUCIFER WE ARE TALKING ABOUT  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /> I read this book solely for the love triangle, because it was one of the best ones out there. I am a little disappointed with the rest of the story truth be told, because it was wayy too predictable. And cheesy. If you are in it for the romance then you will get what you are being promised (AND MORE), but don't try to go too deep because you will find this is the equivalent of a kiddie pool.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9832655033534442467" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/761694626?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer761694626" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17375529610857643821"><b> 3.5 stars </b><br/><br/>Just wanted to reiterate, 3 stars is NOT a bad rating. I liked this book I just didn't love it.<br/><br/><b> Every Last Breath </b> is the conclusion to The Dark Elements series. And while it's not my favorite series by JLA I still thoroughly enjoyed it. This last book just wasn't for me. And it's not because she didn't pick the guy I liked. Or maybe it is? You find out about 20% in and that's not a spoiler because JLA said before she wrote it we would know at the beginning so no fan torture (thank yo</span>
  <span id="freeText17375529610857643821" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 stars </b><br /><br />Just wanted to reiterate, 3 stars is NOT a bad rating. I liked this book I just didn't love it.<br /><br /><b> Every Last Breath </b> is the conclusion to The Dark Elements series. And while it's not my favorite series by JLA I still thoroughly enjoyed it. This last book just wasn't for me. And it's not because she didn't pick the guy I liked. Or maybe it is? You find out about 20% in and that's not a spoiler because JLA said before she wrote it we would know at the beginning so no fan torture (thank you JLA! Much appreciated!)<br /><br /> Honestly, I'm just going to put the entire review in a spoiler tag so read at your own risk.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I was Team Zayne. I also knew she would pick Roth so I was prepared. But as I was reading I found I just didn't care about the characters anymore. Maybe because they got their happy ending mostly at the beginning? Plus I have a VERY hard time with unrequited love. And poor Zayne loved Layla her whole life and not only did he not get the girl, but she literally took away a part of his soul.<br /><br />And on that note it felt like JLA used that as an excuse to make Zayne a jerk in this book. He wasn't there for most of it and he wasn't nice until the end.<br /><br />What I am trying to say and doing a miserable job of is the reason I really liked this series was the anguish that existed between Zayne and Layla not being able to be together. The forbidden love aspect of that. Once it was gone, I wasn't interested in what happened anymore.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Obviously I still enjoyed this book as a 3 on Goodreads means "I liked it". But I guess I was expecting more? What else I couldn't tell you, I just didn't find myself as enraptured in this book like her other series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17375529610857643821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1373417606" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1373417606" />
    <a title="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34403359"><img alt="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469758679p2/34403359.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1373417606?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" href="/user/show/34403359">☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1373417606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3104699094514277897">My goodness. This book was amazing. I have to say that this series gets better as it goes on. There were no disappointments. I don't even know what to write about here. For you to fully understand what I'm going through right now, you'll have to read the series.<br/><br/>So this book starts with the sort of cliffhanger that the Lilin was in someone else's body and that his soul was gone. Through all of the chasing of the Lilin and stopping the apocalypse, Layla has to make her choice of who she'll want to</span>
  <span id="freeText3104699094514277897" style="display:none">My goodness. This book was amazing. I have to say that this series gets better as it goes on. There were no disappointments. I don't even know what to write about here. For you to fully understand what I'm going through right now, you'll have to read the series.<br><br>So this book starts with the sort of cliffhanger that the Lilin was in someone else's body and that his soul was gone. Through all of the chasing of the Lilin and stopping the apocalypse, Layla has to make her choice of who she'll want to be with. She loves both Roth and Zayne but there is only going to be one who she'll be able to spend the rest of her life with.<br><br>Layla has to choose which side she'll be on and which part of her she'll trust. They'll all have to work together to stop the Lilin from continuing the chaos and the war that would kill billions of lives and leave the Earth bare.<br><br>So there were many thing I loved throughout the final installment of Dark Elements.<br><br>1. The characters: I still love Layla and she is even stronger in this one. I remember thinking that she might have been a little weak in the beginning of the series but come on. Who wouldn't be scared when your whole world is changing? Roth *sigh* I loved him even more since he loved Layla. He is so funny and sarcastic yet he can somehow be kind to Layla. Now onto Zayne. I think that my opinion of him has shifted but I don't know how. He's pretty good but I never felt that man-I-really-wish-you-were-real feeling that I had with some other characters. A minor character that I just wanted to mention is Stacey. In my review of White Hot Kiss, I said that I didn't like how she acted as if she was dumb or all over the boys in the school. She definitely "found her lady balls" and accepted whatever was thrown her way, which was a lot more than in the previous books.<br><br>2. The action. There was non-stop action and in the times where there were slight pauses, they were finding new or talking about other problems. And did I mention the plot twists? I was like "Oh no!" and then "YAY!" as I kept reading. You don't know how often I was like:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432490868ra/14971629.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before I realized it was okay. I couldn't rip my eyes from the pages which is exactly what I like.<br><br>3. And last but definitely not least, the ROMANCE! It was so good. Some readers might have decided that it was cheesy but no, no it wasn't. Here is an example:<br><br><i> “I love you,” I told him, and I told him that every day and I would tell him that over and over again.<br><br>[He] lowered his forehead to mine as he brought our joined hands to his chest, placing them above his heart. “And I love you,” he said. “With every breath I take, I will always love you.” </i><br><br>Is that cheesy? I think not<br><br>There was nothing about this book that I didn't like and I'm definitely going to have to reread this series a bazillion more times before I get enough of this. I'm just kidding, that will never happen. I'm most definitely continue reading Ms. Armentrout's wonderful writing as you should too.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3104699094514277897" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31740218-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31740218-jasmine?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31740218-jasmine?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1006395469" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13041003450539521613">So after finishing this book, I don't even know why I liked this series in the first place.<br/>1. It was sappiest thing I've ever read. It was just cringeworthy. <br/><br/>2. I wanted Roth and Layla to be together, and unsurprisingly they were, I just didn't like how it was done. For one, the fact that JLA had people voting for him or Zayne made me feel like no matter what, Layla's choice wouldn't be sincere, just cuz I knew JLA didn't write it based on her characters, but based on a poll. And their relations</span>
  <span id="freeText13041003450539521613" style="display:none">So after finishing this book, I don't even know why I liked this series in the first place.<br />1. It was sappiest thing I've ever read. It was just cringeworthy. <br /><br />2. I wanted Roth and Layla to be together, and unsurprisingly they were, I just didn't like how it was done. For one, the fact that JLA had people voting for him or Zayne made me feel like no matter what, Layla's choice wouldn't be sincere, just cuz I knew JLA didn't write it based on her characters, but based on a poll. And their relationship happened way too early on in the book for my liking. Not only this, but the plot was overshadowed by the romance. It seriously had me wondering if JLA didn't know what to write about and just decided on making the book focused on Roth and Layla instead.<br /><br />3. What little there was of the plot reminded me of Supernatural. But a much crappier Supernatural with a lazy storyline and a cop-out ending so everything can be focused on the romance instead of what's actually going on.<br />I don't even feel like writing more. Didn't like the book. Now that I think of it, I don't care for the series either.<br /><br />*******<br /><br />I need this book so badly I could cry. <br />I need Roth and Layla together so badly that I could cry.<br />I need this book so badly I could cry.<br />If Zayne and Layla end up together, then I, without a doubt, will <i>die.</i><br />And another thing-<br />I need this book so badly that if I don't get it, hunting down JLA and threatening her life seems very realistic.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2161356013245156735">AN EPIC CONCLUSION TO A FANTASTIC SERIES!<br/> <br/><b>“Well, there was only one that I knew I would always be happy with, one that I would always laugh with. One that I did more than long for, but <i>yearned</i> for, and each second that passed ignoring it was a second I wouldn’t get to spend with him- a second I wouldn’t live life with love in it, <i>real</i> love in it, the kind that did have lasting power.”</b><br/> <br/>I’ve not long finished this book and already my mind is reliving my favorites moments, I seriously just want to </span>
  <span id="freeText2161356013245156735" style="display:none">AN EPIC CONCLUSION TO A FANTASTIC SERIES!<br /> <br /><b>“Well, there was only one that I knew I would always be happy with, one that I would always laugh with. One that I did more than long for, but <i>yearned</i> for, and each second that passed ignoring it was a second I wouldn’t get to spend with him- a second I wouldn’t live life with love in it, <i>real</i> love in it, the kind that did have lasting power.”</b><br /> <br />I’ve not long finished this book and already my mind is reliving my favorites moments, I seriously just want to crawl back and read it all over again!!<br /> <br />I’m sure everyone was blown away at the ending of <i>Stone Cold Touch</i>, when we found that our beloved Sam was the Lilin. Every Last Breath picks up from this revelation but now Layla is faced with a haunting decision; she must kill her best friend. The Lilin continues to create havoc in the city and leaving a trail of wraiths in it’s wake, Layla &amp; Co’ know it’s only a matter of time before the Alpha’s intervene and wipe out all Warden and Demon life, resulting in war and eventually the apocalypse.<br /> <br />This book is far from predictable, every time I felt myself becoming familiar with the plot a dramatic twist that you never see coming turns everything upside down… and these twists they just kept coming! I was unable to take my eyes away from the book. There was death, heartbreak, and turmoil, this was a very emotional read!<br /> <br /><b>
  <i>“It’s him. It’s always been him.”</i>
</b><br /> <br />Now for the most important bit of this review as I’m sure you will agree is.. <b>Layla’s decision.</b> I can’t comment much on this as I’m sure you are all aware of what Team I am on and I would never spoil this for you, you really should discover this for yourself.. BUT for those of you who are just dying to see who said this quote look here at the spoiler at your own risk ;)<br /> <br /><b>
  <i>“I’m here… I’m here because this is where I’m happy, with you.”</i>
</b><br /> <br />Roth or Zayne?!&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>ROTH &lt;3</b> I'm so freaking happy about this!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /> <br />AND better yet, I didn’t have to read ¾ of the book for find out who she choose, nope quite early-ish on actually, which allowed me to enjoy the relationship and fangirl but also enjoy the journey. Even with Layla’s important choice the romance was turned up about 70 degrees, I mean this was seriously bringing on a serious blush at times but it was oh soo good. The swoony moments are what I live for and JLA doesn’t disappoint at all. All those silly predictions? Throw those out the window and prepare to be shocked.<br /> <br />To be honest there were some not bad but I'd say repetitive writing/phrases such as: 'rocking in a corner somewhere' or 'I hate to say this'. Also the later plot twist and the ending reminded me of the Covenant series which was a little sad because these are two completely different series however I still loved the book. I was a little baffled by the twist ending as it didn't have the sense of finality and I kept waiting for the other shoe to drop, granted this could have been me having a blonde moment or the affects of reading for too long!<br /><br />I was so impressed by the ending and I'm seriously still a little bit emotional at the shock twist! The blurb did warn us that <i>‘an old bargain comes back to haunt them all.’</i> Haunting isn’t a good enough word for it.. I am crushed, but seriously for you guys who have read this series and loved it, I would scream at you if I could.. You seriously need to read this book, it’s just amazing. The pacing was perfect and packed full of action but as the Queen of romance JLA packs everything in a gorgeously sizzling package. Fellow fans of The Dark Elements.. this is what you’ve been waiting for ;)<br /> <br /><b>
  <i>“I’m pissed off because I love you, Layla, and the idea of losing you fucking terrifies me!”</i>
</b><br /><br /><a href="http://literary-lyobsessed.blogspot.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Literary-ly Obsessed</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2161356013245156735" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1114500778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11287765303116660330">(Edit after reading it at the end of the review)<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403010552ra/10025572.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>OMG JULY 2015, how can we wait that long? <br/><i>White Hot Kiss</i> and <i>Stone Cold Touch</i> were respectively Roth's and Zayne's books. We had two books to choose our team sexy leader, thank you Armentrout. Now, let's try to clear things out: <br/><br/><b>Reasons to root for a Layla-Roth HOT-SEXY-AS-HELL (wink-wink) ending:</b><br/><br/>1)Because Roth is a Disney fan, how cute is that? Because you just can't wait to see Bambi again and to finally meet Thumper. <br/><br/>2)Because his tattoos and hi</span>
  <span id="freeText11287765303116660330" style="display:none">(Edit after reading it at the end of the review)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403010552ra/10025572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OMG JULY 2015, how can we wait that long? <br><i>White Hot Kiss</i> and <i>Stone Cold Touch</i> were respectively Roth's and Zayne's books. We had two books to choose our team sexy leader, thank you Armentrout. Now, let's try to clear things out: <br><br><b>Reasons to root for a Layla-Roth HOT-SEXY-AS-HELL (wink-wink) ending:</b><br><br>1)Because Roth is a Disney fan, how cute is that? Because you just can't wait to see Bambi again and to finally meet Thumper. <br><br>2)Because his tattoos and his rock-hard body have that effect on you:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/522550.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>3)Because he's fighting for you. Despite being chained down by what he IS (a demon, but more than that: THE Crown Prince of Hell for God's sake, talk about responsibilities!) he still doesn't give up on what he wants, on what he doesn't think he deserves but still adores: you.<br><br>4) Because he will get hurt again and again for you. He will do anything to protect you, even if it means watching you being with Stony. He knows what "self-sacrifice" means, and how ironical for a demon, he does it only for you. Again, and again. And again.<br><br>5) Because he's a badass with a foul mouth (that does wonderful thinks on your body <i>hmm</i>). Roth is a real tease that has the grace and power of a predator... a demon pierced in real magical places... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/549902.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6) He won't judge you. You can do anything you want, the more yourself you get, dropping your walls and chains on your way, the more "hot" you become to him. Just be yourself (finally)!<br><br>7) He won't tie you down, he will let you make your mistakes but be right by your side to help or save you at all times. He's not a control-freak, he doesn't think you're a fragile female that needs to be protected and dotted on at all times. You and him, you're a <i>team </i>.<br><br>8) He's the epitome of the bad-boy type, but between his teasing, his smugness and general hotness, he's gentle to you only. Talk about feeling special!<br><br>9) Because even if the Big Boss down there ORDER him to kill you, he can't. He protects and try however he can to save you and let you have a happy life in the bright light of the "good side".<br><br>10) Because he lost himself when he found you.<br><br>Because it's ROTH people, R-O-T-H <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417284528ra/12269746.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Now reasons to be on Team Zayne:</b><br><br>1)Because he's... blond? A Warden? Your kinky brotherly-incest wet dream?<br><br>2)If you're into good-guy. I mean EXTREME good guy. The kind of guy you can lie to, practically cheat on, insult, get cranky and bitchy on his ass and that would still FORGIVE and LOVE YOU because you're just that awesome. Obviously you're not the one in the wrong, it's the whole world that's at fault. No biggie for you, he still worships you.<br><br>3)....Humm...well I got two! It's already a miracle for someone without a personality like him, right?<br><br>...Anyway. <br>J.L. Armentrout has an addictive writing style that make her readers swoon and scream and blush without interruption. Their eyes are glued to her book's line while their emotions are all over the place. And it's good. Handsomely good. I'm like a tree years-old that awaits for her Christmas, I WANT MY <i>Every Last Breath</i>, my heart's crying over here!<br><br>My conclusion?<br><br>Here it is:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/497529.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>Edit after reading the book:</b>
</u><br><br>Just... wow! This final book was amazing! Gontrats Armentrout for no boring down times, there was adventure, suspense, love (maybe a little too much vanilla love, I didn't count how many "I love you"s she wrote but I think I never read so much in one book). <br><br>Honestly, here was my reaction at the end of each chapter:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403308121ra/10074535.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I won't spoil but I'm SO HAPPY with how Lalyla managed her love life! Go girl! <br><br>This whole series was amazing and the ending was awesome and epic! I feared being disappointed but I was so SO wrong!! This book kept me on the edge of my ... bed from the beginning to the end. <br>Thank you JLA for this wonderful series! <br><br><b>I HIGHLY recommend it!!!</b></span>

<div id="review_1128001146" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001146" />
    <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko"><img alt="Katerina  Kondrenko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590049412p2/36306002.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1128001146?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina  Kondrenko" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko">Katerina  Kondrenko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9785170936175" href="/book/show/30319896-kazhdyy-posledniy-vzdoh">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=plot-driven-by-action">plot-driven-by-action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=era-contemp">era-contemp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=ships-not-in-this-harbor">ships-not-in-this-harbor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=pages-301-400">pages-301-400</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=characters-queers">characters-queers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=target-young-adult">target-young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=genre-fantasy">genre-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=pov-1st-person">pov-1st-person</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=friendship-bromance">friendship-bromance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=pov-female-only">pov-female-only</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1128001146" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10399061186207502922"><blockquote>
  <b>1 out of 10</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br/><a href='http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2016/07/every-last-breath-by-jennifer-l.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br/><br/><b>Genre</b>: urban fantasy, YA<br/><b>Stuff</b>: gargoyles, angels, demons<br/><b>Fail</b>: every tiny detail<br/><b>POV</b>: 1st-person, female<br/><b>Love-Geometry</b>: zero<br/><br/><b>Quote-Core</b>: <blockquote>
  
    <i>“You’re like the cute version of the village idiot.”</i>
  
</blockquote><br/>Okay, something did happen with my taste. Only last fall I could tolerate simplicity of JA</span>
  <span id="freeText10399061186207502922" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>1 out of 10</b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br /><a href="http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2016/07/every-last-breath-by-jennifer-l.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br /><br /><b>Genre</b>: urban fantasy, YA<br /><b>Stuff</b>: gargoyles, angels, demons<br /><b>Fail</b>: every tiny detail<br /><b>POV</b>: 1st-person, female<br /><b>Love-Geometry</b>: zero<br /><br /><b>Quote-Core</b>: <blockquote>
  
    <i>“You’re like the cute version of the village idiot.”</i>
  
</blockquote><br />Okay, something did happen with my taste. Only last fall I could tolerate simplicity of JA's books, I understood how unoriginal and meh they were, but it didn't bother the process. Now I just want to kill them all with a fire. Gone blindness before hot guys. Gone fun from witty banters. Gone every JA's book from my TBR.<br /><br />First of all, JA doesn't write fantasy novels, she isn't able to. All her fantasy books are typical romances with alpha guys and virgin TSTL girls. To call love-interests aliens or gargoyles or faeries then make them represent different kinds of exotic creatures and make from an MC a hybrid is not enough for FANTASY novel. Your fucking non-humans should act like non-humans and not like boys-next-door or the-hottest-quarterbacks-ever. You have to build a new world within our own with unique rules and laws. JA never does it. And I'm fed up with her bullshit which is all about abs and sex.<br /><br /><i>Now to the book and its ridiculousness. </i><b>Spoiler alert!</b><br /><br />I won't retell you the plot, just pick out some <u>really stupid things</u> you can find here and in any other JA's works:<br /><br />- A lot of<b> flashbacks</b> and a huge<b> info-dump</b> of the previous events. You can start reading around 50% and nothing would be changed. Actually, you can stop reading at 50% and nothing would be changed too.<br /><br />- <b>Gay-stereotypes</b>. There's a guy, Сayman. And Jen decided to make him the gay guy. I mean, with a passion for fashion, a love for girl-ish talks, and a way to address people with sugar-words. Kiera Cass has the same vision of gays, she and JA have to be friends...<br /><br />- <b>Everyone has to be in a relationship</b>. Cassandra Clare and Sara J. Mass would be proud of Jen Armentrout. In her books you're either dead or in love with somebody. Even familiars (yeah, those animated tattoos) flirt with each other.<br /><br />- <b>Anticlimactic things</b>. Love-triangle, a serious one with all these I-love-them-so-much and I'd-never-be-able-to-choose, was resolved in a matter of seconds at the beginning of the book. Mind that the romance was the driven force of this series. There was no actual plot to be interested in after the girl chose who would have her virginity.<br /><br />- <b>Convenient circumstances</b>. One of the MCs was immortal while the other should grow old and then rest in piece, but BOOM the other MC turned out to be immortal too. Ooookay...<br /><br />- <b>Romance</b>. A mix of NA and teen-ish stuff. MCs do sex, but lack brains. She wonders what he thinks about her, he gets drunk 'cause he's jealous. He orders her around, she finds it sexy. He'd been a very bad boy for ages, she managed to change him. There are tones of declarations of love. And talks about love. And making love. Meh.<br /><br />- <b>The Choice</b>. It's Roth, I'm ok with it, but Leyla says that Zayne has always been just a friend to her, that her feelings weren't romantic at all. Well, yeah, I love making out with my friends too. Nothing romantic. Or logical.<br /><br />- <b>Sex and making out sessions</b>. I've seen the same scenes with the same descriptions before. In JA's books. Copypasting isn't writing...<br /><br />- <b>Nothing makes sense</b>. Angels, demons, gargoyles, witches, apocalypse, school, cartoon characters... everything reminds me of comedies in da American Pie's style. I know, this series isn't about saving the world or a war between different beasts, it's just a crappy romance with super hot teens falling in love forever, but even this kind of books has to have plots and a bit of logic.<br /><br />- <b>No suspense, no worries</b>. In Jen's books MCs never die. Mentors die, bad guys die, random people die, but not MCs. You read with a poker-face and as much poker-heart, 'cause what actully may happen? Somebody breaks a leg? <br /><br />- <b>Attack of the clones</b>. Beautiful girls, handsome boys, tough muscles, round boobs. Hello everyone from Jen's books! No diversity. No personalities. Just good bodies and maidens who have no idea of their perfection.<br /><br /><b>PS</b>: I finished this book only last night and remember next to nothing about the entire series.<br /><b>PPS</b>: Bye JA. Bye forever.<br /><br /><b>The Dark Elements (Тёмные элементы)</b>:<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001108" rel="nofollow noopener">Bitter Sweet Love (Горько-сладкая любовь)</a> #0.5/3<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001208" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot Kiss (Жаркий поцелуй)</a> #1/3<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001130" rel="nofollow noopener">Stone Cold Touch (Холодные объятия)</a> #2/3<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001146" rel="nofollow noopener">Every Last Breath (Каждый вдох)</a> #3/3 </span>
  <a data-text-id="10399061186207502922" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1399949708" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13066464855233456054"><br/><b><blockquote>“I, Astaroth, Crown Prince of Hell, am in love with you, Layla Shaw. Yesterday. Today. Tomorrow. A hudred decades from now, I will still be in love with you, and it will be as fierce today as it will be a decade later.” </blockquote>
<br/><br/>5 Stars!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/roth.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443281055i/16343362._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo roth.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Series:</b> This is the third book in the White Hot Kiss series, and it is the last installment in the trilogy. This series is written by Jennifer L. Armentrout, and it's a fantasy/Romance book that follows Layla, the main character. There is a novella that comes before</span>
  <span id="freeText13066464855233456054" style="display:none"><br><b><blockquote>“I, Astaroth, Crown Prince of Hell, am in love with you, Layla Shaw. Yesterday. Today. Tomorrow. A hudred decades from now, I will still be in love with you, and it will be as fierce today as it will be a decade later.” </blockquote>
<br><br>5 Stars!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/roth.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443281055i/16343362._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo roth.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Series:</b> This is the third book in the White Hot Kiss series, and it is the last installment in the trilogy. This series is written by Jennifer L. Armentrout, and it's a fantasy/Romance book that follows Layla, the main character. There is a novella that comes before this series started, and Jasmine is the lead character. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455585.White_Hot_Kiss__The_Dark_Elements___1_" title="White Hot Kiss (The Dark Elements, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot Kiss</a> is the first, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455815.Stone_Cold_Touch__The_Dark_Elements___2_" title="Stone Cold Touch (The Dark Elements, #2) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Stone Cold Touch</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455817.Every_Last_Breath__The_Dark_Elements___3_" title="Every Last Breath (The Dark Elements, #3) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Every Last Breath</a>, and the novella <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455811.Bitter_Sweet_Love__The_Dark_Elements___0_5_" title="Bitter Sweet Love (The Dark Elements, #0.5) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Bitter Sweet Love</a>.<br><br><b>Story:</b> We follow Layla, after she runs away with Roth from the Wardens. She is still questioning her identity, and her powers. There are two guys who loves her, but she doesn't know who she should choose. This book is action packed with great plot, and hot scenes. It perfectly had all the elements I like in books, and I have to say, I enjoyed it. A lot!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “Cayman cocked his head to the side. “When is there ever a right time to fully give your heart to another? There are always going to be obstacles. You just have to decide which ones are worth it.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>Characters:</b> I really enjoyed the character development in this book. Layla became a badass heroine who protected herself and didn't need to depend on anyone. She faced the hardships she faced without being a coward, which was very very different than how she used to be. Obviously, I like Zayne &amp; Roth. They are both awesome &amp; swoon worthy, but I guess I'm always going to be TeamRoth since they are perfect for each other. I really loved how Roth &amp; Layla had a positive effect on each other. <br><br><b>Side Characters:</b> I honestly liked so many side characters in this book, it was unbelievable. I LOVE Cayman. He was very cute and I wish there was a book in his point of view, I bet he would be a badass. Dez, Jasmine, Danika, and even Abbot were amazing. I even liked the Grim &amp; The Boss! <br><br><b>Ending:</b> HEA! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ ROTH! ROTH! ROTH!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/large.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443281055ra/16343363.gif" alt=" photo large.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “With every breath I take, I will always love you.” <br><br>“You make me wish I had a soul so I could be worthy of you.” </blockquote>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1235025341" />
    <a title="Shannon (kitchandpages)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10961933-shannon-kitchandpages"><img alt="Shannon (kitchandpages)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441470068p2/10961933.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1235025341?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon (kitchandpages)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon (kitchandpages)" href="/user/show/10961933-shannon-kitchandpages">Shannon (kitchandpages)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1235025341" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1829932671866937159">This book was so much fun. I tell myself I'm not going to get sucked into these books because they are silly and a tad ridiculous, but I can't help it. I have pages where I'm rolling my eyes at the cheese and then a page later I'm crying and freaking out. JLA has a way of taking something that could very easily be construed as silly and generic into something sassy, fun and still heartfelt. If you are a fan of her Lux series, or you want something Twilight-Esque but better because of the humor, </span>
  <span id="freeText1829932671866937159" style="display:none">This book was so much fun. I tell myself I'm not going to get sucked into these books because they are silly and a tad ridiculous, but I can't help it. I have pages where I'm rolling my eyes at the cheese and then a page later I'm crying and freaking out. JLA has a way of taking something that could very easily be construed as silly and generic into something sassy, fun and still heartfelt. If you are a fan of her Lux series, or you want something Twilight-Esque but better because of the humor, you should try this series out. They are a fun time :)</span>

<div id="review_2430748128" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2430748128" />
    <a title="Anja H." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h"><img alt="Anja H." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559051853p2/6054186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2430748128?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anja H." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anja H." href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h">Anja H.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781743691113" href="/book/show/25710289-every-last-breath">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2430748128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5178676623306435502"><b>*3.5 DEMONIC STARS*</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You make me wish I had a soul so I could be worthy of you.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>While I loved and enjoyed the previous two books in this trilogy, I kind of expected <i>more</i> from this one.<br/>That ending just seemed too easy and lots of things weren’t explained properly. I kind of expected a big battle in the end but instead it all just felt a bit rushed to me.<br/><br/>Oh well, I still love Roth though. He’s my baby! ❤️</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1138656276" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1138656276" />
    <a title="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3829694-mlpmom-book-reviewer"><img alt="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1375481031p2/3829694.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1138656276?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" href="/user/show/3829694-mlpmom-book-reviewer">Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829694-mlpmom-book-reviewer?shelf=kindle-books">kindle-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1138656276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1959854075379515962">4.5 Stars!<br/><br/>Why does Armentrout always have this amazing ability to draw me into her stories even when those stories make me want to roll my eyes, shake my fist in the air and chuck the book across the room with the nonsense of it all?<br/><br/>I honestly don't know. And even though I know I will more than likely get a headache from all the ups and downs of reading one of her books, I still pick the darn suckers up and dive into the pages.<br/><br/>I don't like so many tropes that her books have, love triangles and a</span>
  <span id="freeText1959854075379515962" style="display:none">4.5 Stars!<br /><br />Why does Armentrout always have this amazing ability to draw me into her stories even when those stories make me want to roll my eyes, shake my fist in the air and chuck the book across the room with the nonsense of it all?<br /><br />I honestly don't know. And even though I know I will more than likely get a headache from all the ups and downs of reading one of her books, I still pick the darn suckers up and dive into the pages.<br /><br />I don't like so many tropes that her books have, love triangles and angst and and and...gah! Some how when I am reading her books. I find myself liking them and enjoying the show. Why is that? It almost sickens me. And yet, she makes it work and she makes me like it. Darn her.<br /><br />I love Layla and Zayne and yes, even Roth. How could I not. Layla is tough and good with a slight bad side to her but most of all she is kick butt and gets things done.<br /><br />Zayne is the ultimate hero and good guy. The kind we all want and then of course Roth is his opposite. A bad boy through and through and yet, he still manages to have some redeeming qualities that make us love him. <br /><br />I absoltuely loved the direction this whole series went, from Layla getting stronger and coming into her own to the direction the friendships and even romance went. It was done so well, so realistically to the story and there were still twists I didn't see coming and things that kept me on my toes.<br /><br />This series like all of Jennifer's writing, was so addictive and I really did have a lot of fun with it, over used tropes, drama, and all. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1959854075379515962" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1085666970" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1085666970" />
    <a title="Maggi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16969868-maggi"><img alt="Maggi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1453844797p2/16969868.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1085666970?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maggi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maggi" href="/user/show/16969868-maggi">Maggi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16969868-maggi?shelf=full-review">full-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1085666970" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer843308811552303143">Okay, here's the thing. I knew from the beginning how I will rate this book, because of the whole <a href='http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/who-will-you-choose/' rel='nofollow noopener'>'Who Will You Choose Thing'</a>.<br/><br/>To summarize it, Armentrout let the reader choose who Layla will end up with. There was a poll, and the guy with the most votes got his happily ever after with Layla.<br/>And she did this, because Jennifer L. Armentrout, the author, creator of this story, didn't know how to decide. She basically had no idea how to solve the love triangle.<br/><br/>Which is just ridiculous.<br/><br/>Let's be serio</span>
  <span id="freeText843308811552303143" style="display:none">Okay, here's the thing. I knew from the beginning how I will rate this book, because of the whole <a href="http://www.jenniferarmentrout.com/who-will-you-choose/" rel="nofollow noopener">'Who Will You Choose Thing'</a>.<br /><br />To summarize it, Armentrout let the reader choose who Layla will end up with. There was a poll, and the guy with the most votes got his happily ever after with Layla.<br />And she did this, because Jennifer L. Armentrout, the author, creator of this story, didn't know how to decide. She basically had no idea how to solve the love triangle.<br /><br />Which is just ridiculous.<br /><br />Let's be serious, she created those characters and the story, she knows them better than anyone, and yet she didn't know who Laylor would 'choose'? What the fuck is this?<br /><br />This is what I call lazy ass writing. She let the readers do her work. Which is unacceptable. <br /><br />Therefore, I just can't give it more than 1 star.<br /><br />There's the question why I did even read it, and truth is, I hate not finishing series. I always want to know how it wrapped up. <br /><br />Now, let's see what I can say about the story itself.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>BEWARE, SPOILERS FOR <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455585.White_Hot_Kiss__The_Dark_Elements___1_" title="White Hot Kiss (The Dark Elements, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot Kiss</a> AND <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455815.Stone_Cold_Touch__The_Dark_Elements___2_" title="Stone Cold Touch (The Dark Elements, #2) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Stone Cold Touch</a></b>
</blockquote><br /><br />It picks up exactly where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17455815.Stone_Cold_Touch__The_Dark_Elements___2_" title="Stone Cold Touch (The Dark Elements, #2) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Stone Cold Touch</a> ended, Layla discovered that Sam, her best friend, is the Lilin. And now she has to kill him to prevent the apocalypse.<br /><br />I can say without doubt that the plot was action-packed and fast-paced, but there was too much romance for my taste. Which is typical for Armentrout's books. <br />So if you liked her Lux series and Covenant series you will definitely enjoy this book. <br /><br />A thing I did like was that the love triangle problem was solved in the first 50 pages. Not too much whining about who she loves more.<br /><br />But I just couldn't stop rolling my eyes. Her characters are so alike. <br />Layla is just another Katy or Alex, Roth another Daemon or Seth. Some of the dialogues were just the same. It's like she just copied and pasted them and changed a few words.<br /><br />Additionally I didn't like the ending, it was too happily ever after for me. <br /><br />Final thoughts:<br /><br />It was a nice wrap-up to the story, if she wouldn't have done the whole 'Who Will You Choose' thing, it would have been a solid 3-stars book. <br />If you're a huge Armentrout fan, go for it. If you think Daemon was kind of an asshole and you're sick of love-triangles, don't even bother.</span>
  <a data-text-id="843308811552303143" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6BazeA0tX4e94aok7cjN8rk8mcbzlODJTCwOtttnxdK4kVktXt4LlElQmHgSTG++2pNQ4r1+I59D9BTnscPPfQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('24thT4PxPlgsE0UNU22jT15ZPVgGRde8EIkLcJwuqjGLDIsa0AJqS9iid1Gs6QEDPfb0fEivFOofUREh9oqgng==')})
  }
//]]>

All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText919624458243725813" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
